		@notify_level_page=0,

		@description=N'No description available.', 
		@category_name=N'[Uncategorized (Local)]', 
		@owner_login_name=N'irpasteam', @job_id = @jobId OUTPUT
IF (@@ERROR <> 0 OR @ReturnCode <> 0) GOTO QuitWithRollback
/****** Object:  Step [Run query]    Script Date: 3/8/2024 7:20:43 PM ******/
EXEC @ReturnCode = msdb.dbo.sp_add_jobstep @job_id=@jobId, @step_name=N'Run query', 
		@step_id=1, 
		@cmdexec_success_code=0, 
		@on_success_action=1, 
		@on_success_step_id=0, 
		@on_fail_action=2, 
		@on_fail_step_id=0, 
		@retry_attempts=0, 
		@retry_interval=0, 
		@os_run_priority=0, @subsystem=N'TSQL', 
		@command=N'Declare @UpdateDate datetime
set @UpdateDate=getdate()

insert into irpas_temp.dbo.BKP_Sec80DPremium
(p.policyid, p.PolicyNo,p.PolicyIssueDate,PolicyEndDate,pp.FinalPremium,pp.Sec80DPremium,ph.PaymentBy,PolicyVersion,UpdateDate)

select top 1000 p.policyid, p.PolicyNo,p.PolicyIssueDate,p.PolicyEndDate,pp.FinalPremium,pp.Sec80DPremium,ph.PaymentBy,p.PolicyVersion,@UpdateDate as UpdateDate  

from tblpolicy(nolock) p
inner join tblPolicyPremium(nolock) pp on p.PolicyID =pp.PolicyID
inner join tblPolicyhealth(nolock) ph on p.PolicyID =ph.PolicyID

 where pp.FinalPremium < pp.Sec80DPremium  and p.PolicyStatusID in (''59'',''1804'')
and Product_ID_PK=''210'' and ph.CoverType=''1'' and p.PolicyEndDate > GETDATE()-1
and p.PolicyVersion=1
order by p.PolicyID desc

Update T set  T.Sec80DPremium = C.FinalPremium
from irpas_temp.dbo.BKP_Sec80DPremium C  , tblPolicyPremium T 
where T.PolicyID = C.PolicyID and C.UpdateDate=@UpdateDate
', 
		@database_name=N'IRPAS', 
		@flags=0
IF (@@ERROR <> 0 OR @ReturnCode <> 0) GOTO QuitWithRollback
EXEC @ReturnCode = msdb.dbo.sp_update_job @job_id = @jobId, @start_step_id = 1
IF (@@ERROR <> 0 OR @ReturnCode <> 0) GOTO QuitWithRollback
EXEC @ReturnCode = msdb.dbo.sp_add_jobschedule @job_id=@jobId, @name=N'Sec80DPremium', 
		@enabled=1, 
		@freq_type=4, 
		@freq_interval=1, 
		@freq_subday_type=1, 
		@freq_subday_interval=0, 
		@freq_relative_interval=0, 
		@freq_recurrence_factor=0, 
		@active_start_date=20200210, 
		@active_end_date=99991231, 
		@active_start_time=500, 
		@active_end_time=235959, 
		@schedule_uid=N'43ec7b20-7935-4396-afdf-64f08f7f718b'
IF (@@ERROR <> 0 OR @ReturnCode <> 0) GOTO QuitWithRollback
EXEC @ReturnCode = msdb.dbo.sp_add_jobserver @job_id = @jobId, @server_name = N'(local)'
IF (@@ERROR <> 0 OR @ReturnCode <> 0) GOTO QuitWithRollback
COMMIT TRANSACTION
GOTO EndSave
QuitWithRollback:
    IF (@@TRANCOUNT > 0) ROLLBACK TRANSACTION
EndSave:
GO

inner join mom.tblMasEmployee tme on us.username = tme.employee_code

		@owner_login_name=N'dbateam', @job_id = @jobId OUTPUT
IF (@@ERROR <> 0 OR @ReturnCode <> 0) GOTO QuitWithRollback
/****** Object:  Step [Index Statistics into Frag table]    Script Date: 3/8/2024 7:20:51 PM ******/
EXEC @ReturnCode = msdb.dbo.sp_add_jobstep @job_id=@jobId, @step_name=N'Index Statistics into Frag table', 
		@step_id=1, 
		@cmdexec_success_code=0, 
		@on_success_action=1, 
		@on_success_step_id=0, 
		@on_fail_action=2, 
		@on_fail_step_id=0, 
		@retry_attempts=0, 
		@retry_interval=0, 
		@os_run_priority=0, @subsystem=N'TSQL', 
		@command=N'--delete from rebuildfrag
  
insert into rebuildfrag(DatabaseName,SchemaName,ObjectName,Index_id, indexName,avg_fragmentation_percent,page_count,IndexType,DateTime)

exec master.sys.sp_MSforeachdb '' USE [?]

SELECT db_name() as DatabaseName, 

QUOTENAME(OBJECT_SCHEMA_NAME(a.object_id, database_id)) schemaName,

OBJECT_NAME (a.object_id) as ObjectName, 

a.index_id, b.name as IndexName, 

avg_fragmentation_in_percent, page_count,index_type_desc,GETDATE() as DateTime

-- , record_count, avg_page_space_used_in_percent --(null in limited)

FROM sys.dm_db_index_physical_stats (db_id(), NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL) AS a

JOIN sys.indexes AS b 

ON a.object_id = b.object_id AND a.index_id = b.index_id



WHERE b.index_id <> 0 and avg_fragmentation_in_percent <>0''
go
 
update rebuildfrag
set Action_Required =''Rebuild''
where avg_fragmentation_percent >25 and page_count>=1000
go

', 
		@database_name=N'DBAAdmin', 
		@flags=0
IF (@@ERROR <> 0 OR @ReturnCode <> 0) GOTO QuitWithRollback

		@enabled=1, 
		@freq_type=4, 
		@freq_interval=1, 
		@freq_subday_type=1, 
		@freq_subday_interval=0,

IF (@@ERROR <> 0 OR @ReturnCode <> 0) GOTO QuitWithRollback
/****** Object:  Step [SCH 1]    Script Date: 3/8/2024 7:21:18 PM ******/
EXEC @ReturnCode = msdb.dbo.sp_add_jobstep @job_id=@jobId, @step_name=N'SCH 1', 
		@step_id=1, 
		@cmdexec_success_code=0, 
		@on_success_action=3, 
		@on_success_step_id=0, 
		@on_fail_action=2, 
		@on_fail_step_id=0, 
		@retry_attempts=0, 
		@retry_interval=0, 
		@os_run_priority=0, @subsystem=N'TSQL', 
		@command=N'insert into irpas_temp.dbo.tblNonActiveUsers
Select ud.UserName,MAX(LogDateTime) as LastLoginDate,UD.UserID,0 isPermissionRemoved,0 UserPermissionCount,0 UserProductPermissionCount,0 UserProductPermissionDetailCount,null RemovedDate  
from tblUserLoginAttemptsLog(nolock) ULA,
Users UD(nolock)
where ULA.UserName=UD.UserName
GROUP BY ud.UserName,UD.UserID
HAVING MAX(LogDateTime)<=DATEADD(YEAR,-1,GETDATE())
order by MAX(LogDateTime) desc
', 
		@database_name=N'IRPAS', 
		@flags=0
IF (@@ERROR <> 0 OR @ReturnCode <> 0) GOTO QuitWithRollback
/****** Object:  Step [Step 2]    Script Date: 3/8/2024 7:21:18 PM ******/
EXEC @ReturnCode = msdb.dbo.sp_add_jobstep @job_id=@jobId, @step_name=N'Step 2', 
		@step_id=2, 
		@cmdexec_success_code=0, 
		@on_success_action=1, 
		@on_success_step_id=0, 
		@on_fail_action=2, 
		@on_fail_step_id=0, 
		@retry_attempts=0, 
		@retry_interval=0, 
		@os_run_priority=0, @subsystem=N'TSQL', 
		@command=N'declare @userId uniqueidentifier,@UserPermissionCount int,@UserProductPermissionCount int,@UserProductPermissionDetailCount int

while (exists(select * from irpas_temp.dbo.tblNonActiveUsers where isnull(isPermissionRemoved,0)=1))
    begin
	   select top 1 @userId=UserID from irpas_temp.dbo.tblNonActiveUsers where isnull(isPermissionRemoved,0)=1


	
	   ----insert into tblUserPermissions(PermissionId,UserID,RoleId,UserorRole,SerialNo,Status,CreatedBy,CreatedDate)
	   ----select PermissionId,UserID,RoleId,UserorRole,SerialNo,Status,CreatedBy,CreatedDate
	   ----from irpas_temp.dbo.tblUserPermissionsD(nolock)
	   ----where UserID=@userId

	   ----insert into tblUserProductPermissions(UserID,ProductID,PermissionID,IsCDTAllowed,BackdationDays,QuoteValidity,IsCDAllowed,PaymentLink,CustomerVerification)
	   ----select UserID,ProductID,PermissionID,IsCDTAllowed,BackdationDays,QuoteValidity,IsCDAllowed,PaymentLink,CustomerVerification
	   ----from irpas_temp.dbo.tblUserProductPermissionsD(nolock)
	   ----where UserID=@userId

	   ----insert into tblUserProductPermissionDetails(UserID,ProductID,PermissionID,Value,RoleId)
	   ----select UserID,ProductID,PermissionID,Value,RoleId
	   ----from irpas_temp.dbo.tblUserProductPermissionDetailsD(nolock)
	   ----where UserID=@userId


	   insert into irpas_temp.dbo.tblUserPermissionsD
	   select *
	   from tblUserPermissions(nolock)
	   where UserID=@userId

	   insert into irpas_temp.dbo.tblUserProductPermissionsD
	   select *
	   from tblUserProductPermissions(nolock)
	   where UserID=@userId

	   insert into irpas_temp.dbo.tblUserProductPermissionDetailsD
	   select *
	   from tblUserProductPermissionDetails(nolock)
	   where UserID=@userId

	   select @UserPermissionCount=COUNT(1)
	   from tblUserPermissions(nolock)
	   where UserID=@userId

	   delete from tblUserPermissions
	   where UserID=@userId

	   select @UserProductPermissionCount=COUNT(1)
	   from tblUserProductPermissions(nolock)
	   where UserID=@userId
	   
	   delete from tblUserProductPermissions
	   where UserID=@userId
	   
	   select @UserProductPermissionDetailCount=COUNT(1)
	   from tblUserProductPermissionDetails(nolock)
	   where UserID=@userId

	   

	   delete
	   from tblUserProductPermissionDetails
	   where UserID=@userId

	   update irpas_temp.dbo.tblNonActiveUsers
	   set isPermissionRemoved=0,UserPermissionCount=@UserPermissionCount,UserProductPermissionCount=@UserProductPermissionCount,UserProductPermissionDetailCount=@UserProductPermissionDetailCount,RemovedDate=GETDATE()
	   where isnull(isPermissionRemoved,0)=1 and userId=@userId

    end

    
UPDATE STATISTICS [tblUserPermissions] with FULLSCAN, maxdop = 0
UPDATE STATISTICS [tblUserProductPermissionDetails] with FULLSCAN, maxdop = 0
UPDATE STATISTICS [tblUserProductPermissions] with FULLSCAN, maxdop = 0


', 
		@database_name=N'IRPAS', 
		@flags=0
IF (@@ERROR <> 0 OR @ReturnCode <> 0) GOTO QuitWithRollback
EXEC @ReturnCode = msdb.dbo.sp_update_job @job_id = @jobId, @start_step_id = 1
IF (@@ERROR <> 0 OR @ReturnCode <> 0) GOTO QuitWithRollback
EXEC @ReturnCode = msdb.dbo.sp_add_jobschedule @job_id=@jobId, @name=N'Sch 2', 
		@enabled=1, 
		@freq_type=4, 
		@freq_interval=1, 
		@freq_subday_type=1, 
		@freq_subday_interval=0, 
		@freq_relative_interval=0,

		@active_start_date=20220716,

,tp.PolicyStartDate,tp.PolicyEndDate ,tp.PolicyIssueDate,us.UserName    INTO tblPaymentlinkReport
from tblPolicy tp (Nolock) inner join Users us (nolock) on tp.CreatedBy = us.UserId
INNER JOIN Applications ap (nolock) on us.ApplicationId = ap.ApplicationId
Inner join MOM.tblMasProduct PD (Nolock) ON tp.Product_ID_PK = PD.Product_ID_PK 
INNER JOIN MOM.tblMasVendor VM (NOLOCK) on tp.AgentID = VM.Vendor_ID_PK

INNER JOIN tblPolicyPremium TPP (NOLOCK) ON tp.PolicyID = tpp.PolicyID 
INNER JOIN tblPolicyPaymentmap PPM (NOLOCK) on tp.PolicyID = PPM.PolicyID 
INNER JOIN tblPaymentInstrumentDetails IPD (Nolock) on PPM.PaymentID = IPD.PaymentID 
LEFT OUTER JOIN tblMAscommontypes tc (nolock) On tp.BusinessTypeId = tc.code  --where MasterType =''BusinessType''
Where ApplicationName =''IMD''
and IPD.PaymentMode =''Online''
and MasterType =''BusinessType''
AND LEN(PolicyNo)=16
and tp.CreatedDate >=''2016-07-01''', 
		@database_name=N'IRPAS',

		@step_id=1, 
		@cmdexec_success_code=0, 
		@on_success_action=1, 
		@on_success_step_id=0,

		@on_fail_step_id=0, 
		@retry_attempts=0, 
		@retry_interval=0, 
		@os_run_priority=0, @subsystem=N'TSQL', 
		@command=N'DECLARE @date DATETIME;
SELECT @date = DATEADD(MM, -1, GETDATE());
SELECT @date;
WHILE
(
    SELECT COUNT(1)
    FROM tbltransactions WITH (NOLOCK)
    WHERE CreatedDate < @date
) > 0
    BEGIN
        SET ROWCOUNT 10000;
        DELETE FROM tbltransactions
        WHERE CreatedDate < @date;
        BREAK;
    END;', 
		@database_name=N'AuditTrail', 
		@flags=0
IF (@@ERROR <> 0 OR @ReturnCode <> 0) GOTO QuitWithRollback

		@enabled=1, 
		@freq_type=8, 
		@freq_interval=1, 
		@freq_subday_type=4, 
		@freq_subday_interval=1, 
		@freq_relative_interval=0,
